add_namespace = ww1_xinhai
add_namespace = ww1_chinaa

# GUANGZHOU UPRISING
#######################
country_event = {
	title = ww1_xinhai.1.t
	desc = ww1_xinhai.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_army_training
	id = ww1_xinhai.1
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_xinhai.1.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100 
		}
		set_global_flag = guangzhou_uprising
		activate_mission_tooltip = CHI_xinhai_revolution_mission
	#	hidden_effect = {
	#		country_event = {
	#			id = ww1_qing.10
	#			days = 17
	#		}
	#	}
	}
}

# XINHAI REVOLUTION STARTS
#############################
country_event = {
	title = ww1_xinhai.2.t
	desc = ww1_xinhai.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	id = ww1_xinhai.2
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = BOX
				}
				remove_core_of = BOX
			}			
			CHI_lu_rongting = {
				set_nationality = CHI
			}
			CHI = {add_ideas = {CHI_uprising}}
						QIN = {add_ideas = {QIN_uprising}}
						QIN = {set_country_flag = revolution_started}			
			XXB = {
						country_event = ww1_china.3
						add_power_balance_value = {
						    id = QIN_centralization_bop
						    value = -0.30
						    tooltip_side = QIN_centralization_bop_democracy
						} 		
			}
			set_global_flag = xinhai_revolution		
			CHI = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = early_infantry_equipment_1 amount = 55000 producer = FRA }
				inherit_technology = QIN
				set_country_flag = beiyang_army

				set_temp_variable = { CHI_tempvar_rebellion_province = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = GUI
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = GUI
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			
				set_cosmetic_tag = BYCH
				set_state_owner = 620
				set_province_controller = 4130
				set_province_controller = 7625
				set_province_controller = 10426
			
promote_character = {
    character = CHI_li_yuanhong
    ideology = neutrality
}				

promote_character = {
    character = CHI_sun_yatsen
    ideology = democratic
}		
promote_character = {
    character = CHI_jiang_kanghu
    ideology = communism
}			
promote_character = {
    character = CHI_jiang_kanghu
    ideology = fascism
}						
				
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = QIN
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = TAN
							is_core_of = TIB
							state = 330
							state = 982
							state = 983
						}
					}
					add_core_of = CHI
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = QIN
					}
					add_claim_by = CHI
				}
				
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
					long_name = CHI_hubei_party
					name = CHI_hubei_party
				}
				set_popularities = {
					fascism = 5
					communism = 0
					democratic = 36
					neutrality = 59
				}
		
				
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = RON_Nationalist_China
					keep_completed = yes
				}

				# Prevents early surrender
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = CHI_idea_revolutionary_fervor
					days = 30 # Maximum time for second revolt to happen: 30 days
				}
			}
			QIN = {
				remove_ideas = QIN_idea_tongmenghui
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = DNC_QIN_continue_imperial_china }
					uncomplete_national_focus = {
						focus = QIN_restore_the_nation
						uncomplete_children = yes
						refund_political_power = no
					}
					mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = QIN_idea_xinhai_revolution
					days = 125
				}
			}
			

			CHI = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = QIN
					type = civil_war
				}
				add_civil_war_target = QIN
				if = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 605
					}
					load_oob = "PRC_1911_Chongqing"
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { 
						owns_state = 599
					}
					load_oob = "PRC_1911_Guangdong"
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { 
						owns_state = 325
					}
					load_oob = "PRC_1911_Yunnan"
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { 
						owns_state = 602
					}
					load_oob = "PRC_1911_Jiangxi"
				}
				else_if = { #Hubei
					limit = { 
						owns_state = 620
					}
					load_oob = "PRC_1911_Wuchang"
				}
				else = {
					load_oob = "PRC_1911_Wuchang"
				}
				
				
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_xinhai_revolution
					
				
			}
			
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = -1.0
			}
			#set_global_flag = QIN_next_uprising
			clr_global_flag = wuchang_uprising
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_xinhai
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.15 #Jingzhou
							days = 3
							random_days = 2
							random_hours = 5
						}
					
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.12 #Hunan
							days = 5
							random_days = 2
							random_hours = 5
						}
					
				
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.13 #Shaanxi
							days = 5
							random_days = 2
							random_hours = 5
						}
					
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.14 #Jiangxi
							days = 8
							random_days = 2
							random_hours = 5
						}
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.16 #Shanxi
							days = 10
							random_days = 2
							random_hours = 5
						}
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.17 #Shanghai --- SETS COSMETIC FLAG
							days = 12
							random_days = 3
							random_hours = 5
						}
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.18 #Yunnan/Guizhou
							days = 10
							random_days = 5
							random_hours = 5
						}
					
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.19 #Zhejiang
							days = 20
							random_days = 6
							random_hours = 5
						}
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.20 #Guangxi
							days = 15
							random_days = 5
							random_hours = 5
						}
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.21 #Sichuan
							days = 40
							random_days = 15
							random_hours = 7
						}
					
						country_event = {
							id = ww1_xinhai.22 #Shandong
							days = 30
							random_days = 10
							random_hours = 9
						}
					}
				}
			
			CHI = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_xinhai } }
					add_named_threat = {
						threat = 5
						name = ww1_xinhai.2.t
					}
					set_global_flag = QIN_flag_first_xinhai
					#set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_revolution
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Support Qing
		name = ww1_xinhai.2.a
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = {
		load_oob = CHI_1914
				load_oob = CHI_1914
				#load_oob = Wuchang_Uprising
				country_event = {
					days = 20
					random_days = 10
					id = ww1_xinhai.3
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = QIN
					type = civil_war
				}
				add_civil_war_target = QIN
				load_oob = "PRC_1911_Wuchang"
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_xinhai_revolution
			}
			set_global_flag = QIN_chosen
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.21
			}
			QIN = {
			change_tag_from = CHI
				if = {
					limit = {
						MON = {
							exists = yes
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = MON
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						TAN = {
							exists = yes
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = TAN
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = qing_chosen
		set_global_flag = QIN_chosen
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Support Chinese Revolution
		name = ww1_xinhai.2.b
		set_global_flag = CHI_chosen
			
	hidden_effect = {
			CHI = {
		load_oob = CHI_1914
				load_oob = CHI_1914
				#load_oob = Wuchang_Uprising
				country_event = {
					days = 20
					random_days = 10
					id = ww1_xinhai.3
				}

				declare_war_on = {
					target = QIN
					type = civil_war
				}
				add_civil_war_target = QIN
				load_oob = "PRC_1911_Wuchang"
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_xinhai_revolution
			}
			set_global_flag = QIN_chosen
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 0.21
			}
			QIN = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						MON = {
							exists = yes
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = MON
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						TAN = {
							exists = yes
						}
					}
					declare_war_on = {
						target = TAN
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = roc_chosen
		#ai_chance = {
		#	factor = 0
		#}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution_ends }
		CHI = {
			exists = yes
		}
date  < 1930.1.1
	}
	
	immediate = {

CCH = {		
		set_state_owner = 602
}
	}
}

	}

		CSH = {

		}
		
		set_global_flag = QIN_third_uprising
		set_global_flag = QIN_first_second_up
		promote_character = CHI_huang_xing
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_revolution
		set_country_flag = second_uprising
		
		QIN = {
			set_country_flag = second_uprising
			CHI_chen_bingkun = {
				set_nationality = CHI
			}
		}
	}
}

#SHIKAI ASKS EMPEROR TO ABDICATE
####################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_xinhai.4
	title = ww1_xinhai.4.t
	desc = ww1_xinhai.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chi_yuan_cabinet
	trigger = {
		tag = QIN
		has_war_with = CHI
		has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution_ends
			has_global_flag = QIN_flag_dont_trigger_xinhai_again
		}
		OR = {
			#has_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_defection
			# we are about to die
			surrender_progress > 0.7
			CHI = { 
				controls_state = 608
			}
			# yuan dont want to waste beiyang troops
			AND = {
				casualties > 100000
				surrender_progress > 0.25
			}
			AND = {
				casualties > 300000
				CHI = { surrender_progress < 0.1 }
			}
			# yuan has another plan :)
			# historical trigger
			AND = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = schemer_yuan
				surrender_progress > 0.10
				NOT = { has_idea = QIN_idea_xinhai_revolution }
				CHI = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_stand_with_tongmenghui
					OR = {
						controls_state = 592
						controls_state = 598
						controls_state = 620
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = CHI_sun_yatsen
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			#AND = {
			#	has_global_flag = QIN_flag_shikai_count_2
			#	fascism > 0.75
			#}
		}
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_yuan_shikai
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_government = neutrality
		has_country_flag = third_uprising
	}
	#fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_xinhai.4.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_dont_trigger_xinhai_again
		remove_ideas = QIN_idea_xuantong_young
		
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_xinhai.4.a.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = { country_event = ww1_xinhai.10 }
			CHI_yuan_shikai = { # no more loyal(ish) prime minister role
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = autocracy
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_xinhai.4.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		trigger = { has_government = neutrality }
		add_war_support = -0.15
		add_stability = -0.15
		add_political_power = -200
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.35
		}
		# clr_global_flag = QIN_flag_beiyang_army_deployed
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Beiyang New Army"
			disband = no
		}
		set_global_flag = QIN_flag_kick_out_shikai
		# custom_effect_tooltip = QIN_effect_cancel_invite_shikai
		CHI_yuan_shikai = {
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				ideology = autocracy
			}
		}
		
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = QIN_neutrality_cabinet_party
			name = QIN_neutrality_cabinet_party
		}
		remove_ideas = QIN_idea_beiyang_army
		transfer_units_fraction = {
			target = CHI
			size = 0.4
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
		}
	}
}

# Mongolian Independence
country_event = {
	id = ww1_xinhai.8
	title = ww1_xinhai.8.t
	desc = ww1_xinhai.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_mongolia_cavalry
	trigger = {
		is_literally_china =  yes
		NOT = { country_exists = MON }
		owns_state = 330
		has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution
		date < 1914.6.1
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_xinhai.8.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_subject = MON
			}
			end_puppet = MON
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_subject = TAN
			}
			end_puppet = TAN
		}
		TAN = {
			transfer_state = 329
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = MON
				}
				transfer_state_to = MON
			}
			MON = {
				country_event = ron_decolonizationdiplo.30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_literally_china =  yes
			}
			add_state_claim = 329
			add_state_claim = 330
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = QIN
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = MON
					type = annex_everything
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = TAN
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_xinhai.8.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_subject = MON
			}
			end_puppet = MON
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_subject = TAN
			}
			end_puppet = TAN
		}
		TAN = {
			transfer_state = 329
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_literally_china =  yes
			}
			add_state_claim = 329
			add_state_claim = 330
			add_state_claim = 982
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = QIN
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = MON
					type = annex_everything
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = TAN
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = MON
				}
				transfer_state_to = MON
			}
	}
}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_chinaa.1.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.1.d
	id = ww1_chinaa.1
	picture = GFX_report_event_chi_yuan_cabinet
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.1.a
		set_global_flag = chinese_warlord_crisis
	#	activate_mission_tooltip = CHI_warlord_era_mission
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_popular_support
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_popular_support
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_popular_support
					}
					AND = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_improved_army_support
						has_idea = CHI_idea_good_popular_support
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = CHI_trait_accepted_monarch
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_trait = unpopular_monarch
		}
	}
}

#WARLORD ERA BEGINS - YUNNAN

country_event = {
	title = ww1_chinaa.2.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.2.d
	id = ww1_chinaa.2
	picture = GFX_report_event_manchukuo_army
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = CHI
			tag = QIN
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		YUN = {
			exists = no
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			YUN = {
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_literally_china =  yes
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								state = 325
							}
						}
						add_core_of = YUN
						YUN = {
							transfer_state = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_tang_jiyao
					}
					CHI_tang_jiyao = {
						set_nationality = YUN
					}
				}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_cai_e
					}
					CHI_cai_e = {
						set_nationality = YUN
					}
				}
				CHI_tang_jiyao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = conservatism
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 6
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = cai_e_dead }
					}
					CHI_cai_e = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = chinese_nationalism }
							promote_character = chinese_nationalism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = chinese_nationalism
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { is_field_marshal = no }
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = CHI
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = CHI
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = CHI
							}
						}
						CHI = {
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 330
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.2.a
	}
}

				}
				set_capital = { state = 608 }
				ROOT = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						limit = {
							has_trait = CHI_loyalist
						}
						set_nationality = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		trigger = { country_exists = QIN }
	}
	picture = QIN_report_event_qing_funeral
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					country_exists = QIN
					country_exists = CHI
				}
			}
			is_literally_china =  yes
		}
		else = {
			has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				CHI = { exists = yes }
				date > 1916.5.1
			}
			date > 1917.8.1
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
				}
				retire_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead }
				}
				CHI = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_completed_focus = CHI_ruling_of_yuan_shikai }
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_completed_focus = CHI_second_empire
								}
							}
							remove_ideas = CHI_idea_republican_plot
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_global_flag = hongxian_failed }
							}
							CHI_beiyang_triumvirate = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = oligarchism
										desc = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate_desc
										traits = { CHI_beiyang_triumvirate }
									}
								}
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = stratocracy
										desc = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate_desc
										traits = { CHI_beiyang_triumvirate }
									}
								}
							}
							CHI_duan_qirui = {
								set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
									slot = political_advisor
									value = no
								}
							}
							activate_advisor = CHI_duan_qirui_political
							CHI_feng_guozhang = {
								set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
									slot = political_advisor
									value = no
								}
							}
							activate_advisor = CHI_feng_guozhang_political
							CHI_wang_shizhen = {
								set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
									slot = political_advisor
									value = no
								}
							}
							activate_advisor = CHI_wang_shizhen_political
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_government = neutrality
								has_elections = yes
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = neutrality
								election_frequency = 60
								elections_allowed = no
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = CHI_idea_hongxian_emperor
						}
						remove_ideas = CHI_idea_hongxian_emperor
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = CHI_idea_stable_republic
						}
						swap_ideas = {
							remove_idea = CHI_idea_stable_republic
							add_idea = CHI_idea_unstable_republic
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
			set_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = yuan_shikai_dead }
				}
				set_country_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
				country_event = ww1_chinaa.10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.10.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = QIN
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = -0.15
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.11
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		CRH = {
			exists = no
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}
	immediate = {
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = {
				has_character = CHI_liu_xianshi
			}
			CHI_liu_xianshi = {
				set_nationality = CRH
			}
		}
		CRH = {
			CHI_liu_xianshi = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = { ideology = despotism }
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = { ideology = stratocracy }
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 603
						}
					}
					add_core_of = CRH
					CRH = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_liu_xianshi
					}
					CHI_liu_xianshi = {
						set_nationality = CRH
					}
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = CHI
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = CHI
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = CHI
							}
						}
						CHI = {
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 330
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.14
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		SHX = {
			exists = no
		}
		OR = {
			country_exists = ANH
			has_global_flag = qing_oppress_cliques
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35
	}
	immediate = {
		SHX = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 615
						}
					}
					add_core_of = SHX
					SHX = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_yan_xishan
				}
				CHI_yan_xishan = {
					set_nationality = SHX
				}
			}
			CHI_yan_xishan = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = conservatism
					}
					promote_character = conservatism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = conservatism
							traits = { king_shanxi propaganda_expert }
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = stratocracy
					}
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
							traits = { king_shanxi propaganda_expert }
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							traits = { king_shanxi propaganda_expert }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			load_oob = CHI_warlord
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
					owner = PREV
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					count = 10
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = ANH
						original_tag = ZHI
					}
				}
				PREV = { give_military_access = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = QIN
				}
				inherit_technology = QIN
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = QIN
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = tech_support
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = QIN
					}
				}
				QIN = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
				else = {
					inherit_technology = ANH
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = ANH
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = ANH
						}
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ANH
						relation = military_access
						active = yes
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ZHI
						relation = military_access
						active = yes
					}
					every_other_country = {
						limit = {
							is_neighbor_of = PREV
						}
						set_truce = {
							target = PREV
							days = 365
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.16
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		FEN = {
			exists = no
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	immediate = {
		SIK = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 287
							state = 618
							state = 749
							state = 894
						}
					}
					add_core_of = SIK
					SIK = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						every_owned_state = {
							set_demilitarized_zone = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 619
						}
					}
					add_core_of = CRH
					CRH = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						every_owned_state = {
							set_demilitarized_zone = no
						}
					}
				}
			}
			982 = {
				add_claim_by = SIK
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_literally_china =  yes }
					}
					330 = {
						owner = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									is_literally_china =  no
								}
								transfer_state = 982
							}
							else = {
								SIK = { transfer_state = 982 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_yang_zengxin
					}
					CHI_yang_zengxin = {
						set_nationality = SIK
					}
				}
				CHI_yang_zengxin = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = despotism traits = { stout_defender } }
					}
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = { ideology = stratocracy traits = { stout_defender } }
					}
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 4
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = CHI
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = CHI
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = CHI
							}
						}
						get_current_government_type = yes
						CHI = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = PREV
								autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
							}
						}
						restore_previous_government_type = yes
					}
				}
				CRH = { get_current_government_type = yes }
				set_autonomy = {
					target = CRH
					autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
				}
				CRH = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
			}

				}
				every_owned_state = {

							state = 622
							# state = 942
							state = 890
						}
					}
					add_core_of = CSY
					transfer_state_to = CSY
				}
			}

				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 4
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {
						inherit_technology = ANH
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 5000
							producer = ANH
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_tech = tech_support
							}
							add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
								type = support_equipment
								amount = 500
								producer = ANH
							}
						}
						ANH = {
							set_truce = {
								target = PREV
								days = 330
							}
							# puppet shaanxi (Chen Shufan)
							if = {
								limit = { country_exists = CSY }
								CSY = { get_current_government_type = yes }
								set_autonomy = {
									target = CSY
									autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
								}
								CSY = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		SHX = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 622
							state = 942
							state = 890
						}
					}
					add_core_of = SHX
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 942
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = SHX
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 2
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = QIN
					}
					inherit_technology = QIN
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 5000
						producer = QIN
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_tech = tech_support
						}
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = support_equipment
							amount = 500
							producer = QIN
						}
					}
					QIN = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
					else = {

	}

						}

				load_oob = CHI_warlord

							}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_chinaa.30.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.30.d
	id = ww1_chinaa.30
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_global_flag = CHI_government_split_mission
		NOT = { country_exists = ANH }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_duan_qirui
				}
				CHI_duan_qirui = {
					set_nationality = ANH
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_xu_shichang
				}
				CHI_xu_shichang = {
					set_nationality = ANH
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_lin_jianzhang
				}
				CHI_lin_jianzhang = {
					set_nationality = ANH
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_duan_zhigui
				}
				CHI_duan_zhigui = {
					set_nationality = ANH
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
				}
				CHI_feng_guozhang = {
					set_nationality = ZHI
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_cao_kun
				}
				CHI_cao_kun = {
					set_nationality = ZHI
				}
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_du_xigui
				}
				CHI_du_xigui = {
					set_nationality = ZHI
				}
			}
			ANH = {
				CHI_duan_qirui = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = oligarchism
						}
						promote_character = oligarchism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				inherit_technology = CHI
				set_research_slots = 3
				annex_country = {
					target = CHI
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_neutrality
				if = {
					limit = {
						CHI = { has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president }
					}
					meta_effect = {
						text = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = neutrality
								last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
								election_frequency = 60
								elections_allowed = no
							}
						}
						CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
					}
					add_ideas = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president
					else = {
						add_ideas = CHI_idea_xu_shichang_president
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = CHI
						is_core_of = QIN
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ANH
				# STOP RELEASE DAMN CHINA
				remove_core_of = CHI
				remove_core_of = QIN
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_claimed_by = CHI
						is_claimed_by = QIN
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = ANH
				remove_claim_by = CHI
				remove_claim_by = QIN
			}
			ZHI = {
				CHI_cao_kun ={
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = oligarchism
						}
						promote_character = oligarchism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
				}
				CHI_feng_guozhang = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = oligarchism
						}
						promote_character = oligarchism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = { ideology = oligarchism }
						}
					}
				}
				inherit_technology = CHI
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OWNER = {
							is_literally_china =  yes
							OR = {
								is_subject = no
								AND = {
									is_subject = yes
									OVERLORD = { is_literally_china =  no }
								}
							}
						}
						OR = {
							#Zhili
							state = 614
							#Shandong
							state = 597
							state = 597
							#Henan
							state = 607
							state = 891
							#Jiangsu
							state = 598
							#Hubei
							state = 620
							#Jiangxi
							state = 600
						}
					}
					add_core_of = PREV
					transfer_state_to = PREV
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_neutrality
				every_owned_state = {
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_literally_china =  yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = PREV }
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 143
							region = 144
							region = 164
						}
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							tag = ZHI
						}
						to_state = 614
					}
				}
			}
			ANH = {
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = ZHI
					size = 0.5
					stockpile_ratio = 0.5
					army_ratio = 0.5
					navy_ratio = 0.5
					air_ratio = 0.5
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
						always = yes
					}
				}
				set_capital = { state = 608 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = FEN
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							region = 155
						}
						add_core_of = FEN
						transfer_state_to = FEN
						set_demilitarized_zone = no
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_literally_china =  yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = PREV }
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 143
							region = 144
							region = 164
						}
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							tag = ANH
						}
						to_state = 608
					}
				}
				change_tag_from = CHI
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.30.a
	}
}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_chinaa.31.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.31.d
	id = ww1_chinaa.31
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_running
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.31.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
		FROM = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					tag = XSM
					tag = SHX
					tag = GXC
					tag = SIK
					tag = YUN
					tag = CSD
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 70
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.31.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_subject_of = FROM }
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = ww1_chinaa.32
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				FROM = { has_government = neutrality }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_major = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 70
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.31.c
		FROM = {
			country_event = ww1_chinaa.34
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

# UNITED CHINA - SHARE PROBLEMS WITH WARLORDS
##################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.35
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		is_chinese_warlord = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = part_of_china }
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = MAN
			}
			NOT = { is_subject_of = JAP }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	immediate = {
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_neutrality
		set_country_flag = part_of_china
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = yes
				OVERLORD = { has_country_flag = part_of_china }
			}
			copy_warlord_problem = yes
			add_ideas = CHI_ineffective_bureaucracy_warlord
			add_ideas = PRC_government_corruption
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_illiteracy
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_weak_industry
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation5
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation4
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation3
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation2
						has_idea = CHI_idea_inflation
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_inflation5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = CHI_idea_army_corruption3
						has_idea = CHI_idea_army_corruption2
						has_idea = CHI_idea_army_corruption
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_army_corruption
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_ineffective_bureaucracy_warlord
			add_ideas = PRC_government_corruption
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_illiteracy
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_weak_industry

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = MAN_banditry
						has_idea = CHI_idea_merchant_army
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_banditry
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						num_of_factories > 4
						tag = FEN
						tag = GXC
						tag = ANH
						tag = ZHI
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_rampant_opiate_addiction
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	title = ww1_chinaa.37.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_chinaa.37.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = CHI_kuomintang
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_chinaa.37.d_yatsen
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = CHI_kuomintang
		}
	}
	id = ww1_chinaa.37
	picture = GFX_report_event_manchukuo_army
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			leave_faction = yes
			set_rule = {
				can_join_factions = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = CHI_kuomintang
				}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = CHI
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 0
						neutrality = 47
						fascism = 53
						communism = 0
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
					set_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
					reserve_dynamic_country = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							region = 143
							region = 145
							region = 155
							region = 200
							state = 607
						}
						NOT = {
							state = 615
							state = 622
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = NPA
				}
				NPA = {
					set_capital = { state = 608 }
					inherit_technology = CHI
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = fascism
						long_name = CHI_neutrality_party
						name = CHI_neutrality_party
					}
					set_rule = {
						can_join_factions = no
					}
					add_ideas = CHI_idea_army_corruption
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
				}
				CHI_duan_qirui = {
					set_nationality = NPA
				}
				CHI_li_yuanhong = {
					set_nationality = NPA
				}

					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead }
					}
					CHI_yuan_shikai = {
						set_nationality = NPA
					}
				}
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = NPA
					size = 0.5
					stockpile_ratio = 0.4
					army_ratio = 0.5
					navy_ratio = 0.3
					air_ratio = 0.45
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
						OR = {
							is_character = CHI_yan_xishan
							is_character = CHI_cai_e
							is_character = CHI_chen_jiongming
							has_trait = chinese_nationalist
							has_trait = chinese_federalist
							NOT = {
								has_trait = yuan_shikai_loyalist
								has_trait = chinese_royalist
							}
						}
					}
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = yuan_shikai_loyalist
					}
					set_nationality = NPA
				}
				add_ideas = standing_alone
				complete_national_focus = CHI_focus_national_protection_war
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				NPA = {
					CHI_duan_qirui = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = oligarchism
							}
						}
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}
						}
					}
					CHI_li_yuanhong = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							promote_leader = yes
							country_leader = {
								ideology = oligarchism
							}
						}
					}
					complete_national_focus = CHI_focus_national_protection_war
					mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
					add_ideas = standing_alone
					uncomplete_national_focus = {
						focus = CHI_kuomintang
						uncomplete_children = yes
						refund_political_power = no
					}
					unlock_national_focus = CHI_ruling_of_yuan_shikai
					unlock_national_focus = CHI_replace_governors
					unlock_national_focus = CHI_reorganization_loans
					unlock_national_focus = CHI_expand_state_arsenals
					unlock_national_focus = CHI_increase_army_influence
					unlock_national_focus = CHI_presidential_loyalty
					unlock_national_focus = CHI_suppress_nationalists
					unlock_national_focus = CHI_parliament_liquidation
					unlock_national_focus = CHI_maintain_status_quo
					mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = CHI
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 31
						neutrality = 63
						fascism = 4
						communism = 2
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = NPA
					set_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
					reserve_dynamic_country = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 325
							# state = 591
							# state = 592
							# state = 593
							# state = 594
							# state = 599
							# state = 602
							# state = 603
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = NPA
				}
				NPA = {
					set_capital = {
						state = 325
					}
					inherit_technology = CHI
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = neutrality
						long_name = CHI_national_protection_army_long
						name = CHI_national_protection_army
					}

	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.39.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_chinaa.39.b.tt
		declare_war_on = {
			target = GXC
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = { add_ideas = CHI_idea_sun_yatsen_president }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = GXC
					NOT = {
						tag = GXC
						has_war_with = CHI
						is_subject_of = CHI
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = GXC
					enemy = CHI
				}
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_sun_yatsen_president
			}
		}
		GXC = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

				limit = {

					NOT = { state = 599 }

				add_core_of = CLS

					limit = {
						owner = {
							is_literally_china =  yes
						}
						OR = {
							state = 592
							state = 892
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = CLS
				}
			}
			CHI = {
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_secure_internal_politics
				unlock_national_focus = CHI_focus_align_with_guangzhou_government
				#unlock_national_focus = CHI_cooperation_with_the_nationalists

				# load_focus_tree = china_warlord_focus

					inherit_technology = GXC
					else = {

							limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }

						}

								country_leader = {
									ideology = tridemism
									traits = { chinese_nationalist father_of_the_republic }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						CHI_wang_jingwei = {
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
								promote_character = tridemism
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									promote_leader = yes
									country_leader = {
										ideology = tridemism
										traits = { chinese_nationalist }
									}
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
								promote_character = reformist_socialism
							}
							else = {

									}
									promote_leader = yes
								}
							}
						}

					}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.50
	title = ww1_chinaa.50.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.50.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting

	# 						ideology = stratocracy
	# 					}
	# 				}
	# 			}
	# 		}
	# 	}
	# }
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.50.a
		set_global_flag = second_zhili_fengtian_war
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ZHI
			type = annex_everything
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			set_faction_name = anti_zhili_alliance
		}
		else = {
			create_faction = anti_zhili_alliance
		}
		add_to_faction = ANH
		
		# if = {
		# 	limit = {
		# 		any_other_country = {

		# 		country_event = ww1_chinaa.51
		# 	}
		# }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.50.b
		add_war_support = -0.15
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = ROOT

				is_owned_by = ZHI
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

				}

					}

				add_claim_by = FEN
			}

		}

# DEATH OF SUN YAT-SEN
#########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.54
	title = ww1_chinaa.54.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_chinaa.54.d
		trigger = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_chinaa.54.d_alt
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = xinhai_revolution } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
		date > 1925.3.1
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 12
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
				}
				retire_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
						has_character = CHI_hu_hanmin
					}
					CHI_hu_hanmin = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
							promote_character = tridemism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = tridemism
									traits = { conservative_nationalist }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
					suspend_elections = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
			set_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = sun_yatsen_dead }
				}
				set_country_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
				country_event = ww1_chinaa.54
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.54.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag }
				promote_character = CHI_hu_hanmin
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = communism
				has_country_leader_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.54.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_sun_yatsen
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = democratic
				has_government = communism
				has_country_leader_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
			}
		}
	}
}

# COMMUNIST PARTY OF CHINA

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.57
	title = ww1_chinaa.57.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.57.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	trigger = {
		date > 1919.1.1
		is_literally_china =  yes
		OR = {
			country_exists = SOV
			has_global_flag = october_revolution
			has_global_flag = french_civil_war
			has_global_flag = CHI_may_fourth_movement
			any_other_country = {
				is_major = yes
				has_government = communism
			}
			communism > 0.50 #manual override
		}
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party
		}
		# on chinese mainland
		capital_scope = {
			OR = {
				region = 143
				region = 144
				region = 164
				region = 165
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 100 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = chinese_communist_party
			set_country_flag = chinese_communist_party
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = CHI_idea_communist_movement
				days = 365
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_ideology = anarchist_communism
						has_country_leader_ideology = syndicalism
						has_global_flag = french_civil_war
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = communism
					long_name = CHI_syndicalist_party_long
					name = CHI_syndicalist_party
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = communism
					long_name = CHI_communist_party_long
					name = CHI_communist_party
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					NOT = {
						original_tag = PRC
						has_country_flag = chinese_communist_party
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				country_event = ww1_chinaa.57
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_li_dazhao
				}
				CHI_li_dazhao = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						 promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = vanguardism
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_government = communism } }
					CHI_li_dazhao = { promote_character = vanguardism }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.57.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = communism }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.57.b
		trigger = {
			has_government = communism
		}
	}
}

# CHINESE SOVIET REPUBLIC

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.58
	title = ww1_chinaa.58.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.58.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		is_literally_china =  yes
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_global_flag = chinese_soviet_republic
			any_country = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_united_front
			}
			any_country = {
				is_literally_china =  yes
				has_government = communism
			}
		}
		owns_state = 600
		any_owned_state = {
			is_core_of = CHI
			NOT = { state = 600 }
		}
		OR = {
			date > 1931.11.1
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
			communism > 0.3
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = chinese_soviet_republic
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CHI_idea_communist_movement
				}
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_communist_movement
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CHI_idea_united_front
				}
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_united_front
			}
			PRC = {
				add_state_core = 600

				# set_cosmetic_tag = CJS

						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV

				}

				set_country_flag = part_of_china
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_warlord_neutrality
				add_ideas = CHI_ineffective_bureaucracy_warlord
				add_ideas = PRC_government_corruption
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_illiteracy
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_weak_industry
				add_ideas = CHI_banditry
				add_ideas = CHI_rampant_opiate_addiction
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.58.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		CJS = {
			every_neighbor_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
						is_in_faction_with = PREV
						is_subject_of = PREV
					}
				}
				PREV = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#add_civil_war_target = CJS
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.58.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		CJS = {
			every_neighbor_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
						is_in_faction_with = PREV

				}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.60
	title = ww1_chinaa.60.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.60.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_fighting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = CXZ
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
					has_country_flag = CHI_zhigongdang_flag
					has_cosmetic_tag = GXC_TWN
				}
			}
			white_peace = CXZ
			set_truce = {
				target = CXZ
				days = 180
			}
			set_country_flag = zhili_fengtian_fengyushang_war_participants
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = CSD
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
					has_country_flag = CHI_zhigongdang_flag
					has_cosmetic_tag = GXC_TWN
				}
			}
			white_peace = CSD
			set_truce = {
				target = CSD
				days = 180
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = CAH
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
					has_country_flag = CHI_zhigongdang_flag
					has_cosmetic_tag = GXC_TWN
				}
			}
			white_peace = CAH
			set_truce = {
				target = CAH
				days = 180
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = FEN
					is_owned_by = CXZ
				}
				OR = {
					region = 144
					region = 164
					region = 165
				}
			}
			ZHI = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX = { has_country_flag = zhili_fengtian_fengyushang_war_participants }
			}
			every_state = {

# MANCHURIAN INCIDENT
#########################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.65
	title = ww1_chinaa.65.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.65.t
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# trigger = {
	# 	OR = {
	# 		has_country_flag = reunited_china
	# 		has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
	# 		AND = {
	# 			tag = SHX
	# 			has_global_flag = anti_chiang_war
	# 			has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_united
	# 		}
	# 	}
	# 	is_in_faction_with = FEN
	# 	JAP = {
	# 		has_war_with = FEN
	# 	}
	# }
	# mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	# fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			GXC = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_global_flag = anti_chiang_war
						has_cosmetic_tag = TWN_GUANGZHOU
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = warlord_era_end
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = reunite_china
						country_exists = CHI
					}
					any_country = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					add_to_faction = FEN
					set_country_flag = manchurian_incident
				}
				FEN = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = CHI
						enemy = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = anti_chiang_war
					SHX = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_united
					}
				}
				SHX = {
					add_to_faction = FEN
					set_country_flag = manchurian_incident
				}
				FEN = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = SHX
						enemy = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = reunite_china
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = reunited_china
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = CHI_soviet_republic_flag
								has_country_flag = CHI_left_kuomintang_flag
								has_country_flag = long_march_end
								has_cosmetic_tag = TWN_BEIPING
								has_cosmetic_tag = QIN_government
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
							set_faction_name = chinese_salvation_army
							else = {
								create_faction = chinese_salvation_army
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = communism
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
							set_faction_name = chinese_red_army
							else = {
								create_faction = chinese_red_army
							}
						}
					}
					add_to_faction = FEN

							}

								country = PREV

								active = yes

						}

		}
	}
	option = {

		}
	}

						OR = {
tag = CHI
tag = CHI
}
						has_country_flag = reunited_china
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				any_enemy_country = {
					OR = {
tag = CHI
tag = CHI
}
				}
				surrender_progress > 0.3
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

			}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						OR = {
tag = CHI
tag = CHI
}
						AND = {
							is_subject = yes
							OVERLORD = {
								OR = {
tag = CHI
tag = CHI
}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_in_faction = yes
							any_allied_country = {
								OR = {
tag = CHI
tag = CHI
}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				white_peace = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 603 }

					owner = {
						transfer_state = 603
					}
				}
			}

					target = ROOT

			}
		}

# DEATH OF FENG GUOZHANG

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.68
	title = ww1_chinaa.68.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_chinaa.68.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				country_exists = CHI
				AND = {
					country_exists = ZHI
					country_exists = ANH
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_chinaa.68.d2
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_chinaa.68.d3
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	trigger = {
		date > 1919.4.1
		has_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 12 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
				}
				retire_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
			}
			set_country_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
			set_global_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = feng_guozhang_dead
				country_event = ww1_chinaa.68
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.68.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_feng_guozhang
		}
		add_political_power = -75
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			set_country_flag = duan_qirui_president
			set_country_flag = chinese_government_crackdown
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = ROOT
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						election_frequency = 60
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				# prepare government divide
				ANH = {
					meta_effect = {
						text = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = neutrality
								last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
								election_frequency = 60
								elections_allowed = no
							}
						}
						CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
					}
					# Duan is president, no need to add ideas
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.69
	title = ww1_chinaa.69.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.69.t
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_literally_china =  yes
				has_war_with = CHI
			}
			white_peace = CHI
		}
		SHX = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CHI
				}
				add_core_of = SHX
				remove_core_of = CHI
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = CHI
				}
				add_claim_by = SHX
				remove_claim_by = CHI
			}
			CHI = {
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = PREV.PREV
				}
				transfer_navy = {
					target = PREV
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = PREV
					}
					remove_core_of = PREV
					add_core_of = SHX
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = PREV
					}
					remove_claim_by = PREV
					add_claim_by = SHX
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = CHI
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			set_capital = {
				state = 608
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = TWN_BEIPING
			set_truce = {
				target = FEN
				days = 300
			}
			add_to_faction = FEN
			set_global_flag = warlord_era_end
			change_tag_from = CHI
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.69.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

				target = ROOT
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}

# WANG JINGWEI AND GUANGZHOU GOVERNMENT
##########################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.72
	title = ww1_chinaa.72.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.72.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.72.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = CHI_idea_constitutional_movement }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = CHI_idea_constitutional_movement
				add_idea = CHI_idea_nationalist_revolution
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = reunited_china
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 598
				}
				hidden_effect = { set_capital = { state = 598 } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = TWN_NANJING
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 620
				}
				hidden_effect = { set_capital = { state = 620 } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = TWN_WUHAN
			}
			else = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = TWN_GUANGZHOU
			}
		}
		CHI_wang_jingwei = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
				promote_character = tridemism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = tridemism
						traits = { chinese_nationalist }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_chiang_kaishek = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
				promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						traits = { chinese_nationalist generallissimo }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = CHI_revolutionary_army_long
			name = CHI_revolutionary_army
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.81
	title = ww1_chinaa.81.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.81.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_idea = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
		has_global_flag = duan_qirui_great_war
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	# Send Zhang Xun to Beijing
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.81.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		add_stability = 0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_chinaa.146
				days = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	# Side with Li Yuanhong
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.81.b
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = CHI_li_yuanhong
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FEN
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 328
							state = 717
						}
					}
					add_core_of = FEN
					transfer_state_to = FEN
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = fascism
			size = 0.5
			states = {
				595
				596
				597
				597
				606
				607
				609
				610
				611
				614
				617
				619
				716
				597
			}
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					is_character = QIN_zhang_xun
					is_character = CHI_duan_qirui
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = ANH
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
				name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
			}
			PREV = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = li_yuanhong_in_charge
					}
					PREV = {
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = PREV
							size = 0.2
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				democratic > 0.40
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				fascism < 0.05
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# DEATH OF CAI E
###########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.82
	title = ww1_chinaa.82.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.82.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_funeral
	trigger = {
		date > 1916.11.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
			}
			NOT = { original_tag = QIN }
			is_literally_china =  yes
			owns_state = 608
		}
		else = {
			has_character = CHI_cai_e
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 8 }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_cai_e
				}
				retire_character = CHI_cai_e
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
				}
				CHI_tang_jiyao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				CHI_liang_qichao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
						promote_character = reformist_socialism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = reformist_socialism
								traits = { gentle_scholar }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = conservatism
								traits = { gentle_scholar }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = cai_e_dead
			set_country_flag = cai_e_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = cai_e_dead }
				}
				set_country_flag = cai_e_dead
				country_event = ww1_chinaa.82
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.82.a
		add_political_power = -75
	}
}

# CHINISE UNITED FRONT IN WARLORD ERA
########################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.83
	title = ww1_chinaa.83.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.83.d
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		date > 2000.1.1
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			is_in_faction = no
		}
		OR = {
			any_other_country = {
				is_literally_china =  no
				is_major = yes
				NOT = { tag = SIK }
				NOT = { tag = MON }
				NOT = { tag = TIB }
				has_offensive_war_with = PREV
			}
			AND = {
				any_other_country = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					is_subject = no
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = PREV
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							PREV = {
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
						has_government = communism
						else = {
							NOT = {
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
					}
					any_other_country = {
						is_literally_china =  no
						is_major = yes
						has_offensive_war_with = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.83.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		# FLAGS
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = chinese_salvation_army
			set_country_flag = chinese_salvation_army_leader
		}
		# CREATE FACTION
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			create_faction = chinese_salvation_army
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = chinese_salvation_army_reserve
				}
				set_faction_name = chinese_salvation_army
			}
		}
		# INVITE OTHER CHINESE COUNTRIES
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_literally_china =  yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = PREV
					is_in_faction_with = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						PREV = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
					has_government = communism
					else = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = ww1_chinaa.84
		}
		# GOOD EFFECTS
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.83.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.89
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					tag = CHI
					tag = QIN
				}
				OR = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = no
						NOT = {
							has_global_flag = warlord_era
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_literally_china =  yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = reunited_china
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
			has_war_with = FRA
			is_in_faction_with = FRA
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GER
			#GER = {
			#	has_completed_focus = GER_chinese_intervention
			#}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = PREV
				NOT = {
					is_subject_of = PREV
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					has_war_with = FRA
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			add_to_faction = PREV
		}
	}
}

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = HOI4TGW_Opinion_influence_faction
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
		}
		FROM = {
			add_political_power = 30
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PREV
				modifier = HOI4TGW_Opinion_influence_faction
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = PREV
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
			add_to_faction = PREV
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				has_country_leader_with_trait = chinese_federalist
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = CHI_zhao_hengti
						ruling_only = yes
					}
					has_country_leader = {
						character = SIK_sheng_shicai
						ruling_only = yes
					}

						character = CHI_tang_jiyao
						ruling_only = yes
					}

						character = ZHC_wu_peifu

					}

			add_war_support = 0.05
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PREV
				modifier = HOI4TGW_Opinion_diplomats_malus
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_government = communism
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_government = fascism
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10

}

		}

			}

		}

			ideology = communism
			popularity = -0.30
		}

			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_other_country = {

							character = CHI_li_dazhao
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				retire_character = CHI_li_dazhao
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_li_dazhao
					}
					retire_character = CHI_li_dazhao
				}
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {

				is_major = yes
				has_government = communism
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT

	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	# trigger = {
	# 	tag = CHI
	# 	has_war = no
	# 	has_global_flag = manchu_restoration
	# 	is_subject = no
	# 	NOT = { country_exists = QIN }
	# }
	# fire_only_once = yes
	# mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = QIN_zhang_xun
				}
				retire_character = QIN_zhang_xun
			}
			set_capital = { state = 608 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.112.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		add_popularity = {

		}

			set_country_flag = new_assembly
		}
	}
	option = {

		custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_chinaa.112.b.tt
		add_popularity = {

			popularity = 0.10
