				id = ww1_chinaa.113
				days = 10
			}
			set_country_flag = old_assembly
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# Presidential Problem
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.113
	title = ww1_chinaa.113.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.113.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Side with Duan Qirui
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.113.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			promote_character = CHI_duan_qirui
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = neutrality
				size = 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FEN
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_literally_china =  yes }
						OR = {
							state = 328
							state = 717
						}
					}
					add_core_of = FEN
					transfer_state_to = FEN
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SIK
					country_exists = CRH
				}
				SIK = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CRH
						autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
					}
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
				name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = neutrality
				size = 0.35
				states = {
					238
					598
					600
					608
					612
					613
					615
					616
					620
					621
				}
				keep_political_party_members = yes
				PREV = {
					CHI_li_yuanhong = {
						set_nationality = PREV.PREV
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_trait = chinese_federalist
								has_trait = chinese_nationalist
							}
							NOT = { is_character = CHI_yan_xishan }
						}
						set_nationality = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
				promote_character = CHI_li_yuanhong
				CHI_li_yuanhong = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = conservatism
						}
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising_alt
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Side with Li Yuanhong
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.113.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			promote_character = CHI_li_yuanhong
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = fascism
				size = 0.5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising_alt
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				dismantle_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = FEN
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						owner = { is_literally_china =  yes }
						OR = {
							state = 328
							state = 717
						}
					}
					add_core_of = FEN
					transfer_state_to = FEN
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = { end_puppet = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = SIK
					country_exists = CRH
				}
				SIK = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CRH
						autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
					}
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			promote_character = CHI_li_yuanhong
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = fascism
				size = 0.5
				states = {
					595
					596
					597
					597
					606
					607
					609
					610
					611
					614
					617
					619
					716
					597
				}
				keep_political_party_members = yes
				PREV = {
					CHI_duan_qirui = {
						set_nationality = PREV.PREV
					}
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = chinese_federalist
							has_trait = chinese_nationalist
						}
						NOT = { is_character = CHI_yan_xishan }
					}
					set_nationality = PREV.PREV
				}
				promote_character = CHI_duan_qirui
				CHI_duan_qirui = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
					name = CHI_neutrality_anfu_party
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = ANH
				PREV = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = li_yuanhong_in_charge
						}
						PREV = {
							transfer_units_fraction = {
								target = PREV
								size = 0.2
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# Empire of China is falling apart
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.117
	title = ww1_chinaa.117.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.117.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_global_flag = national_protection_war
		has_capitulated = no
		NOT = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = communism
		}
		any_other_country = {
			original_tag = CHI
			has_war_with = PREV
			has_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = lu_rongting_npa
				ROOT = { surrender_progress > 0.30 }
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.117.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		CHI_army_support_decrease = yes
		CHI_duan_qirui = {
			remove_unit_leader_trait = yuan_shikai_loyalist
		}
		CHI_feng_guozhang = {
			remove_unit_leader_trait = yuan_shikai_loyalist
		}
		activate_decision = CHI_sue_for_peace_NPA
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.117.b
		add_stability = -0.25
		add_war_support = -0.25
		custom_effect_tooltip = ww1_chinaa.117.b.tt
		CHI_army_support_decrease = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_chinaa.118
				days = 10
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# Back to Republic?
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.121
	title = ww1_chinaa.121.t
	desc = {
		text = ww1_chinaa.121.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				CHI_yuan_keding = {
					skill > 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ww1_chinaa.121.d2
		trigger = {
			CHI_yuan_keding = {
				skill > 1
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_character = CHI_yuan_keding
		has_completed_focus = CHI_second_empire
		has_global_flag = yuan_shikai_dead
		has_global_flag = national_protection_war
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = NPA
			country_exists = NPA
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 0 }
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.121.a
		retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
		set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
		retire_character = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		CHI_duan_qirui = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
				promote_character = oligarchism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = oligarchism
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
				promote_character = stratocracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = stratocracy
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_li_yuanhong = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
				promote_character = oligarchism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = oligarchism
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_rule = {
			can_not_declare_war = yes
			can_join_factions = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_duan_qirui = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_feng_guozhang = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_wang_shizhen = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			unlock_national_focus = CHI_beiyang_meditator
			set_global_flag = chinese_warlord_crisis
			set_global_flag = warlord_era
			country_event = ww1_chinaa.2
			#set_country_flag = chinese_government_crackdown
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
			set_capital = { state = 608 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
					}
				}
				CHI_sun_yatsen = {
					promote_character = tridemism
				}
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 40
				neutrality = 50
				fascism = 8
				communism = 2
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_chinaa.98
			days = 10
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				GER = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.121.b

					original_tag = QIN

		}

# Cai E Restores Democracy 
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.122
	title = ww1_chinaa.122.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.122.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	trigger = {
		tag = CHI
		has_global_flag = national_protection_war
		has_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
			has_government = fascism
			has_country_flag = lu_rongting_npa
			has_global_flag = hongxian_failed
		}
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.122.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = CHI_cai_e
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = standing_alone
		set_cosmetic_tag = NPA_government
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = QIN_progressive_party_long
				name = QIN_progressive_party
			}
			CHI_liang_qichao = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
					promote_character = reformist_socialism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = reformist_socialism
							traits = { gentle_scholar }
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_liang_qichao = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
				promote_character = conservatism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = conservatism
						traits = { gentle_scholar }
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					long_name = QIN_progressive_party_long
					name = QIN_progressive_party
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		set_country_flag = national_protection_government
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.122.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = CHI_cai_e
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = NPA_government
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = chinese_communist_party }
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = QIN_progressive_party_long
				name = QIN_progressive_party
			}
			CHI_liang_qichao = {

				}
			}

				is_core_of = CHI

					region = 200
				}
			}

			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

					character = FEN_zhang_zuolin
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

		add_stability = -0.10

# DEATH OF HUANG XING
#########################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.129
	title = ww1_chinaa.129.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.129.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
			}
			is_literally_china =  yes
			owns_state = 608
		}
		else = {
			has_character = CHI_huang_xing
			NOT = { original_tag = QIN }
		}
		date > 1916.10.1
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 31
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_huang_xing
				}
				retire_character = CHI_huang_xing
			}
			set_country_flag = huang_xing_dead
			set_global_flag = huang_xing_dead
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					NOT = { has_country_flag = huang_xing_dead }
				}
				set_country_flag = huang_xing_dead
				country_event = ww1_chinaa.129
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.129.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_character = CHI_huang_xing
		}
	}
}

# End of Beiyang Triumvirate
## This for when Yuan Shikai died without declaring the empire
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.131
	title = ww1_chinaa.131.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.131.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_officers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.131.a
		retire_character = CHI_beiyang_triumvirate
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
		CHI_duan_qirui = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
				promote_character = oligarchism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = oligarchism
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
				promote_character = stratocracy
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = stratocracy
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		CHI_li_yuanhong = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
				promote_character = oligarchism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = oligarchism
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_rule = {
			can_not_declare_war = yes
			can_join_factions = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_duan_qirui = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_feng_guozhang = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_wang_shizhen = {
				set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
					slot = political_advisor
					value = yes
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = chinese_warlord_crisis
			set_global_flag = warlord_era
			country_event = ww1_chinaa.2
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
			set_capital = { state = 608 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead
					}
				}
				CHI_sun_yatsen = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
						promote_character = tridemism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = tridemism
								traits = { chinese_nationalist father_of_the_republic }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 40
				neutrality = 50
				fascism = 8
				communism = 2
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
			unlock_national_focus = CHI_beiyang_meditator
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_chinaa.98
			days = 10
		}
	}
}

			date > 1922.3.20

		}
	}

		CHI_tang_jiyao = {
			promote_character = stratocracy
			promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
		}
	}
}

		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				fascism > 0.10
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				fascism > 0.30
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.143.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				democratic > 0.25
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				democratic > 0.60
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ww1_chinaa.145
	title = ww1_chinaa.145.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.145.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SWI_assembly_hall
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = {
			character = CHI_li_yuanhong
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_government = neutrality
		has_civil_war = no
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_idea = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			has_idea = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			has_global_flag = constitutional_protection_war
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.145.a
		add_stability = 0.10
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				neutrality > 30
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				neutrality > 60
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				neutrality > 80
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.145.b
		add_stability = 0.10
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		# Li Yuanhong clique transfered to democratic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.30
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CHI_idea_beiyang_government }
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_beiyang_government
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CHI_idea_beiyang_government2 }
				remove_ideas = CHI_idea_beiyang_government2
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = CHI_neutrality_progressive_party
				name = CHI_neutrality_progressive_party
			}
			CHI_li_yuanhong = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = conservatism
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				democratic > 10
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				democratic > 30
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				democratic > 60
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				democratic > 80
			}
		}
	}
}

# Li Yuanhong Presidency ended
## This is needed when if the Great War is over before Duan's demand to join the war
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.153
	title = ww1_chinaa.153.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.153.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.153.a
		hidden_effect = {
			ANH = {
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = neutrality
							last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
							election_frequency = 60
							elections_allowed = no
						}
					}
					CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
				}
				# Duan is president, no need to add ideas
			}
			set_country_flag = chinese_government_crackdown
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = feng_guozhang_dead }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
					add_idea = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_president
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_li_duan_conflict
		}
		CHI_duan_qirui = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
				promote_character = oligarchism
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						ideology = oligarchism
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		meta_effect = {
			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = ROOT
					last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
		}
	}
}

# NPA Victorious
##############################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.154
	title = ww1_chinaa.154.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.154.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_infiltration
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 31
					neutrality = 63
					fascism = 4
					communism = 2
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = CHI_national_protection_army_long
					name = CHI_national_protection_army
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = CHI_national_protection_army_long
					name = CHI_national_protection_army
				}
				NPA = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_core_of = PREV
								is_claimed_by = PREV
							}
						}
						remove_core_of = PREV
						remove_claim_by = PREV
					}
					transfer_navy = {
						target = CHI
					}
					every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
					CHI_cai_e = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
					CHI_sun_yatsen = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
					CHI_tang_jiyao = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
					CHI_liang_qichao = {
						set_nationality = CHI
					}
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = NPA
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				retire_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
				retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = yuan_shikai_loyalist
					}
					remove_unit_leader_role = yes
				}
				CHI_tang_jiyao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
						promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = authoritarian_democracy
								traits = { chinese_federalist }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
						promote_character = stratocracy
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = stratocracy
							}	
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = cai_e_dead }
					}
					CHI_cai_e = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = chinese_nationalism }
							promote_character = chinese_nationalism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = chinese_nationalism
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy }
							promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = authoritarian_democracy
									traits = {
										revolutionary_general
										generallissimo
									}
								}	
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { is_field_marshal = no }
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				CHI_liang_qichao = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_ideology = conservatism }
						promote_character = conservatism
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								ideology = conservatism
								traits = { gentle_scholar  }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_global_flag = sun_yatsen_dead }
					}
					CHI_sun_yatsen = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = tridemism }
							promote_character = tridemism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = tridemism
									traits = { chinese_nationalist father_of_the_republic }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_ideology = reformist_socialism }
							promote_character = reformist_socialism
						}
						else = {
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = {
									ideology = reformist_socialism
									traits = { chinese_nationalist father_of_the_republic }
								}
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = NPA
				set_country_flag = CHI_national_protection_flag
				change_tag_from = NPA
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.154.a
		remove_ideas = standing_alone
		add_stability = 0.10
	}
}

	desc = ww1_chinaa.155.d

						}

					remove_core_of = PREV

				}
				retire_character = CHI_cai_e
				transfer_navy = {
					target = CHI
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
				# CHI_cai_e = {
				# 	set_nationality = CHI
				# }
				CHI_sun_yatsen = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
				CHI_tang_jiyao = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
				CHI_liang_qichao = {
					set_nationality = CHI
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = NPA
				transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		remove_ideas = standing_alone

			popularity = 0.10
		}

		}
	}

	id = ww1_chinaa.157
	title = ww1_chinaa.157.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.157.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FEN
		owns_state = 608
		has_global_flag = northern_expedition
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
			has_government = communism
		}
		any_other_country = {
			is_literally_china =  yes
			has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
			OR = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
				has_war_with = ZHI
				has_war_with = ANH
				has_war_with = CAH
				has_war_with = CSD
				any_other_country = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.157.a
		set_global_flag = national_pacification_army
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			set_faction_name = national_pacification_army
			else = {
				create_faction = national_pacification_army
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = CHI_idea_duan_qirui_executive
			}
			remove_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui_executive
			add_country_leader_trait = generallissimo
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.170
	title = ww1_chinaa.170.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.170.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.170.a
		CHI = {
			annex_country = {
				target = TIB
				transfer_troops = no
			}
			add_manpower = -100000
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_1
				amount = -2500
				producer = CHI
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					set_rule = {
						can_join_factions = yes
					}
				}
				FRA = {
					add_to_faction = CHI
				}
			}
			else = {
				CHI = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ENG
						relation = guarantee
						active = yes
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ENG
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
				}
				ENG = {
						diplomatic_relation = {
						country = CHI
						relation = guarantee
						active = yes
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = CHI
						relation = non_aggression_pact
						active = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

				has_idea = idea_armistice

			}
		}

				country_exists = TIB
			}

				target = TIB
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = take_claimed_state
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

					tag = FROM
					ratio < 1.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_support < 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with_major = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.171.b
		add_political_power = -50
		add_war_support = -0.15
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
	}

# China - Question of the Constitution
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.174
	title = ww1_chinaa.174.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.174.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.174.e
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.174.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution
			add_idea = CHI_idea_monarchist_constitution
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_monarchist_constitution
		}
		CHI_popular_support_increase = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.174.b
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution
			add_idea = CHI_idea_military_constitution
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_military_constitution
		}
		CHI_army_support_increase = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.174.c
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution
			add_idea = CHI_idea_absolute_constitution
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_idea = CHI_idea_yuan_constitution }
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_absolute_constitution
		}
		CHI_popular_support_decrease = yes
		CHI_army_support_decrease = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}
}

		tag = CCH

			ruling_only = yes
		}
		#CCH_tan_yankai = {
		#	has_trait = chinese_nationalist
		#}
		any_neighbor_country = {
			OR = {
tag = CHI
tag = CHI
}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 180
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.182.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			check_democratic_civil_war_popularity = yes
			set_global_flag = hunan_civil_war
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = democratic
			size = civil_war_size_var
			states = { 893 }
			keep_political_leader = yes
			keep_political_party_members = yes
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = chinese_federalist
					has_trait = politically_connected
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = part_of_china
				#PREV = {
				#	CCH_tan_yankai = {
				#		set_nationality = PREV.PREV
				#	}
				#}
			#	promote_character = CCH_tan_yankai
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
					name = CHI_kuomintang_party
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_zhao_hengti
				}
				CHI_zhao_hengti = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
}

	}
	fire_only_once = yes

		remove_puppet_and_leave_faction = yes
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
			name = CHI_kuomintang_party
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
			name = CHI_kuomintang_party
		}
		#CCH_tang_shengzhi = {
		#	add_country_leader_role = {
		#		promote_leader = yes
		#		country_leader = {
		#			ideology = conservatism
		#			traits = { chinese_nationalist }
		#		}
		#	}
		#	add_country_leader_role = {
		#		promote_leader = yes
		#		country_leader = {
		#			ideology = authoritarian_democracy
		#			traits = { chinese_nationalist }
		#		}
		#	}
		#}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_popularities = {
			democratic = 40
			neutrality = 60
		}
		CHI = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			effect_tooltip = {
				puppet = ROOT
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				ROOT = { get_current_government_type = yes }
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
					end_wars = no
					end_civil_wars = no
				}
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						add_to_war = {
							targeted_alliance = CHI
							enemy = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 602
			}
			620 = {
				owner = {
					set_state_controller = 602
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# May Fourth Movement
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.192
	title = ww1_chinaa.192.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.192.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		is_literally_china =  yes
		controls_state = 608
		has_global_flag = great_war_ends
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 1910.4.1
				date < 1911.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1911.4.1
				date < 1912.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1912.4.1
				date < 1913.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1913.4.1
				date < 1914.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1914.4.1
				date < 1915.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1915.4.1
				date < 1916.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1916.4.1
				date < 1917.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1917.4.1
				date < 1918.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1918.4.1
				date < 1919.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1919.4.1
				date < 1920.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1920.4.1
				date < 1921.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1921.4.1
				date < 1922.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1922.4.1
				date < 1923.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1923.4.1
				date < 1924.6.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1924.4.1
				date < 1925.6.1
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			owns_state = 597
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					has_war_with = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		any_country = {
			has_country_flag = accepted_twenty_one_demands
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.192.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = CHI_may_fourth_movement
			days = 60
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = CHI_may_fourth_movement
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_literally_china =  yes
					NOT = { has_idea = CHI_may_fourth_movement }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_chinaa.193
					hours = 10
				}
			}
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_chinaa.194
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = ww1_chinaa.194.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {

				set_country_flag = rejected_twenty_one_demands
			}
		}
	}

			has_idea = CHI_may_fourth_movement
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.194.b
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 597
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.194.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 597
				has_idea = CHI_may_fourth_movement
			}
		}
	}

# Provisional Chief Executive
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.195
	title = ww1_chinaa.195.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.195.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.195.a
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui_executive
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = ANH }
				ANH = {
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_core_of = ANH
								is_claimed_by = ANH
							}
						}
						remove_core_of = ANH
						remove_claim_by = ANH
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_exists = FEN
						}
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									state = 329
									state = 330
									state = 982
								}
							}
							transfer_state_to = FEN
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = FEN
							size = 0.5
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
						transfer_navy = {
							target = FEN
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							country_exists = ZHI
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = ZHI
							size = 1.0
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = ANH
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
			# rest in peace
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = ANC_xu_shuzheng }
				retire_character = ANC_xu_shuzheng
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = ANC_duan_zhigui }
				retire_character = ANC_duan_zhigui
			}
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { has_character = ANC_ni_sichong }
				retire_character = ANC_ni_sichong
			}
			# move
			#every_possible_country = {
			#	limit = { has_character = ANC_qu_tongfeng }
			#	ANC_qu_tongfeng = {
			#		set_nationality = ROOT
			#	}
			#}
			#every_possible_country = {
			#	limit = { has_character = ANC_wu_guangxin }
			#	ANC_wu_guangxin = {
			#		set_nationality = ROOT
			#	}
			#}
		}
	}
}

# Zhang Zongchang's Shandong - CZL
# Shandong-Zhili Army 直魯聯軍
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.197
	title = ww1_chinaa.197.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.197.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = FEN
		owns_state = 597
		NOT = {
			country_exists = CZL
			has_global_flag = qing_oppress_cliques
			has_country_flag = reunited_china
			owns_state = 598
		}
		has_global_flag = warlord_era
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CZL = {
				add_state_core = 597
				add_state_core = 745
				add_state_core = 746
				add_state_core = 597
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						OR = {
							state = 614 #zhili
							state = 597
							state = 745
							state = 746
							state = 597
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = PREV
					set_demilitarized_zone = no
				}
				#every_possible_country = {
				#	limit = {
				#		has_character = FEN_zhang_zongchang
				#	}
				#	FEN_zhang_zongchang = { set_nationality = CZL }
				#}
				#FEN_zhang_zongchang = {
				#	add_country_leader_role = {
				#		promote_leader = yes
				#		country_leader = {
				#			ideology = despotism
				#			traits = { tyrant lunatic }
				#		}
				#	}
				#	add_country_leader_role = {
				#		promote_leader = yes
				#		country_leader = {
				#			ideology = stratocracy
				#			traits = { tyrant lunatic }
				#		}
				#	}
				#}
				every_possible_country = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_zhang_huaizhi
					}
					retire_character = CHI_zhang_huaizhi
				}
				load_oob = CHI_warlord
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Juntuán\"	start_experience_factor = 0.4	start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = PREV
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						count = 10
					}
				}
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = tech_support
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = ROOT
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_ai = yes
							has_army_size = { size > 20 }
						}
						transfer_units_fraction = {
							target = CZL
							size = 0.2
							air_ratio = 0
							navy_ratio = 0
							stockpile_ratio = 0
							keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
								always = yes
							}
						}
					}
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CZL
						autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
					}
					copy_government_of_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.197.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			release_puppet = CZL
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.197.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		effect_tooltip = {
			release_puppet = CZL
		}
		CZL = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

tag = CHI
tag = CHI
}
			has_government = democratic
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
		NOT = { owns_state = 890 }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 180
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.204.a

				transfer_state = 622
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.204.b
		890 = {
			owner = {

					create_wargoal = {

# Guangxi Overthrown
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.211
	title = ww1_chinaa.211.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.211.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GXC
		has_war = no
		is_subject = no
	#	#is_literally_china = no
		OR = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				original_tag = CLS
				has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
				any_enemy_country = {
					original_tag = CLS
					has_country_flag = CHI_zhigongdang_flag
				}
			}
			has_global_flag = yung_feng_incident
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = neutrality
			has_government = fascism
		}
		#has_character = GXC_li_zongren
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 40
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.211.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = CHI_lu_rongting }
			CHI_lu_rongting = {
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = despotism
				}
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = stratocracy
				}
				remove_unit_leader_role = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = CHI_chen_bingkun }
			CHI_chen_bingkun = {
				remove_unit_leader_role = yes
			}
		}
		retire_character = GXC_tan_haoming
		add_country_leader_trait = chinese_nationalist
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_trait = politically_connected }
			add_trait = {
				trait = chinese_nationalist
			}
		}
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = neutrality 
			long_name = CHI_kuomintang_party_long
			name = CHI_kuomintang_party
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = GXC_TWN
		#GXC_li_zongren = {
		#	promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
		#}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					OR = {
tag = CHI
tag = CHI
}
					AND = {
						is_subject = yes
						OVERLORD = {
							OR = {
tag = CHI
tag = CHI
}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		#	GXC_li_zongren = {
		#		promote_character = stratocracy
		#	}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 30
				neutrality = 60
				fascism = 0
				communism = 10
			}
			get_current_government_type = yes
		}
		CHI = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = ROOT
				autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_regional_government
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.211.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		#retire_character = GXC_li_zongren
		retire_character = GXC_bai_chongxi
	}
}

# NPA denounces the Truce
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.215
	title = ww1_chinaa.215.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.215.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.215.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = {
					has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = CHI_yuan_shikai
					}
					CHI_yuan_shikai = {
						set_portraits = {
							civilian = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/CHI/CHI_yuan_shikai.png"
							}
							army = {
								large = "gfx/leaders/CHI/CHI_yuan_shikai.png"
							}
						}
						set_character_name = CHI_yuan_shikai
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = oligarchism
						}
						remove_country_leader_role = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
						remove_unit_leader_role = yes
					}
				}
			}
			retire_character = CHI_yuan_keding
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_uprising
			set_capital = {
				state = 608
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = CHI_fascism_party
				name = CHI_fascism_party
			}
			CHI_duan_qirui = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_unit_leader = yes
						is_field_marshal = no
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
					promote_character = oligarchism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = oligarchism
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = stratocracy }
					promote_character = stratocracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = stratocracy
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			CHI_li_yuanhong = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = oligarchism }
					promote_character = oligarchism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							ideology = oligarchism
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CHI_idea_unstable_republic
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_popularities = {
			democratic = 40
			neutrality = 50
			fascism = 8
			communism = 2
		}
		set_rule = {
			can_not_declare_war = yes
		}
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_duan_qirui
		add_ideas = CHI_idea_feng_guozhang_vice_president
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_chinaa.98
			days = 10
		}
		set_stability = 0.30
		set_war_support = 0.25
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.217.b
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_chinaa.218
				hours = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

# Chiang Kai-shek almost got killed
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.222
	title = ww1_chinaa.222.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.222.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin
	trigger = {
		is_literally_china =  yes
		has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
		has_character = CHI_chiang_kaishek
		CHI_chiang_kaishek = {
			OR = {
				is_leading_army = yes
				is_leading_army_group = yes
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = northern_expedition
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = CAH
			has_war_with = ZHI
		}
		any_state = {
			OR = {
				region = 144
				region = 164
			}
			owner = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.222.a
		add_war_support = -0.10
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.222.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				surrender_progress > 0.10
				NOT = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = CHI_chiang_kaishek
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = -0.30
		retire_character = CHI_chiang_kaishek
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = -0.10
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					communism > 0.15
					has_idea = CHI_idea_united_front
				}
			}
			CHI_wang_jingwei = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = tridemism
					}
					promote_character = tridemism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = tridemism
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = reformist_socialism
					}
					promote_character = reformist_socialism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = reformist_socialism
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			CHI_hu_hanmin = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = tridemism
					}
					promote_character = tridemism
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = tridemism
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy
					}
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						promote_leader = yes
						country_leader = {
							ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# End of Northern Expedition
country_event = {
	id = ww1_chinaa.223
	title = ww1_chinaa.223.t
	desc = ww1_chinaa.223.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_city_ruin
	trigger = {
		is_literally_china =  yes
		has_country_flag = CHI_kuomintang_flag
		has_global_flag = northern_expedition
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
			any_enemy_country = {
				is_literally_china =  yes
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_chinaa.223.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = end_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = CXZ
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 607
						state = 890
						state = 891
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = CXZ
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = SHX
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 608
						state = 609
						state = 611
						state = 614
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = SHX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GXC
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					region = 165
				}
				transfer_state_to = GXC
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 598
				has_country_leader = {
					character = CHI_chiang_kaishek
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_capital = {
				state = 598
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = TWN_NANJING
		}
		else = {
			set_capital = {
				state = 620
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = TWN_WUHAN
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader_with_trait = chinese_nationalist
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_to_faction = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = northern_expedition_end
			news_event = {
				id = ww1_chinaa.61
				hours = 3
			}
		}
	}
}
